The platform is self service and extremely easy to use. The quality of advertisers that use Impact Radius far exceeds those on other networks, <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">There is nothing that I dislike strongly however I do wish that customer service was a little more hands on when submitting tickets.
